		760 = { add_core_of = NFA }
        34 = { transfer_state_to = NFA }
		6 = { transfer_state_to = NFA }
		29 = { transfer_state_to = NFA }

NFA_establish_rk_TUS = {
	icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 162
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}

	available = {
		162 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = NFA is_subject_of = NFA } } }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	complete_effect = {
		release = TUS
		TUS = {
			every_core_state = {
				remove_core_of = TUS
			}
		}
		162 = { add_core_of = TUS }

		TUS = { 
			every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { 
							is_core_of = NFA
						}
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = NFA
							OWNER = { is_subject_of = NFA} 
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = TUS
			}
		}
		TUS = { 
			set_cosmetic_tag = NFA_TUS_OCC
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus            

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Giuseppe Ferdinando I"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TUS/Portrait_TUS_Giuseppe_Ferdinando.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = maurrassism_subtype
				traits = {
				}
			}

			set_popularities = {
				syndicalist = 5.0
				social_democrat = 5.0
				social_liberal = 0.0
				market_liberal = 0.0
				social_conservative = 20.0
				authoritarian_democrat = 50.0
				paternal_autocrat = 10.0
				national_populist = 10.0
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = "Action Francaise"
				long_name = "Action Francaise"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				name = "Action Francaise"
				long_name = "Action Francaise"
			}

			NFA = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = TUS
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_populist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
	}
}
